// These are special base actors for Remixer monsters, miscellaneous characters,
// and other actors that require them for one reason or another. Because
// of how certain monsters need to be inherited to use their special functions,
// these bases are pretty much copied from the generic monster bases with changes
// needed to get them running. Note that if the generic monster bases are updated,
// then the special bases will also have to be updated.

// Hexen - Dragon - SamsaraMonsterBeastTotalGib
Actor SamsaraMonsterRemixDragon : Dragon
{
	DamageFactor "CorvusCrossbow", 1.1
	DamageFactor "DragonClaw", 1.5
	DamageFactor "WitchMelee", 1.1
	DamageFactor "DeusExSabot", 0.8
	DamageFactor "DeusExSabotPistol", 0.8
	PainChance "MightyBoot", 256
	PainChance "CalebFire", 0
	PainChance "WTMelee", 256
	PainChance "WTMeleeIce", 256
	PainChance "DoomDamageTypeStunner", 256
	PainChance "Shock", 256
	PainChance "Tesla", 256
	+NOICEDEATH
	var int user_scalex;
	var int user_scaley;
	var int user_scalexoriginal;
	var int user_scaleyoriginal;
	States
	{

// Hexen - Zedek - SamsaraMonsterHumanoidMedium
Actor SamsaraMonsterRemixFighterBoss : FighterBoss
{
	DamageFactor "CorvusCrossbow", 1.1
	DamageFactor "DragonClaw", 1.5
	DamageFactor "WitchMelee", 1.1
	DamageFactor "DeusExSabot", 0.8
	DamageFactor "DeusExSabotPistol", 0.8
	PainChance "MightyBoot", 256
	PainChance "CalebFire", 0
	PainChance "WTMelee", 256
	PainChance "WTMeleeIce", 256
	PainChance "DoomDamageTypeStunner", 256
	PainChance "Shock", 256
	PainChance "Tesla", 256
	+NOICEDEATH
	var int user_scalex;
	var int user_scaley;
	var int user_scalexoriginal;
	var int user_scaleyoriginal;
	States
	{
		// Pain states
		Pain.DoomDamageTypeStunner:
			"####" "#" 2 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",true)
			"####" "#" 300 A_Pain
			"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",false)
			"####" "#" -1 A_Jump(256,"See")
			Wait

// Hexen - Traductus - SamsaraMonsterHumanoidMedium
Actor SamsaraMonsterRemixClericBoss : ClericBoss
{
	DamageFactor "CorvusCrossbow", 1.1
	DamageFactor "DragonClaw", 1.5
	DamageFactor "WitchMelee", 1.1
	DamageFactor "DeusExSabot", 0.8
	DamageFactor "DeusExSabotPistol", 0.8
	PainChance "MightyBoot", 256
	PainChance "CalebFire", 0

	PainChance "WTMeleeIce", 256
	PainChance "DoomDamageTypeStunner", 256
	PainChance "Shock", 256
	PainChance "Tesla", 256
	+NOICEDEATH
	var int user_scalex;
	var int user_scaley;
	var int user_scalexoriginal;
	var int user_scaleyoriginal;
	States
	{
		// Pain states
